 abhinayta-nirdeshak pi samutiraqni ne twit kiya, "kisi ko maansik sudhaar or ilaaj kii jarurat he
 Unnecessary attempts to harm the name and respect of actors and actresses
 soshal media kaa sahi istemaal karen
 "comments 10
 Actor Vishal, president of the South Indian Artists Association, said, ‚Äúthe videos and photos posted are fake
 ham pataa laga rahe hai ki inhen kisne aplod kiya he
 Suchitra is undergoing treatment
 " Dhanush has recently finished shooting for the film Power Pindi, he directed this film
 in dinon vah apni saali or rajnikant kii beti saundarya ke nirdesan main ban rahi viipi 2 kii shooting main vyast hai
 Actress Kajol is also playing an important role in this film
 1
 In late February, Suchitra's Twitter handle posted a photo of a scratch in her hand
 is twit main dhanush ke suraksha gardon par suchithra se galat vyavhaar kaa aarope lagaaya gaya
 He wrote in the tweet, "I am Sochi, i came back
 main surakshit hum or sabko bataanaa chaahati hum ki dhanush ne kaisaa ganda khel khelaa he
 "subsequently, several personal photos of the actors were posted from Suchitra's Twitter handle last week with the # Suchileaks hashtag
 inamen dhanush, trisha krishnan, aaraje chinmayi or hansika motwani kii tasviren shaamil thim
 2
 baad main ye tasviren delit kar di gayi or ek tivi channel se baatchat main suchithra ne kaha, "meraa twitor acount hack ho gaya he or mujhe nahin pataa tha ki mere pej par sitaron kii privet tasviren share kii gai hai
 Dhanush's friend Aditi Ravichandran informed me about this on Friday morning
 maine is maamle main jaanch ke liye ek privet investigator hair kiya he
 "later some more photos were shared
 3
 In some tweets, Suchitra also indirectly accused her colleagues of casting couch
 4
 Suchitra's husband Karthik, who is a stand up comedian and actor, posted a video on his Facebook page saying that the account has not been hacked
 unhone kaha, "yah darshata he ki vah kis bhaavnaatmak sthiti main hai or parivaar main ham sabhi unhen is sthiti se ubarne main harsambhav koshish kar rahe hai
 "he requested the media to treat Suchitra as any family member does
 baad main vah video hataa diya gaya
 5
 karthik ke is video kii jagah unke fasebuk pej par ek post share kiya gaya jisamen unhone kaha, "parivaar ke taur par pichley kuch din hamaare liye kaaphi mushkil rahe kyonki suchithra kaa twitor acount hack kar diya gaya tha
 Today we have retrieved their account
 pichley kuch dinon main unke acount se jo bhi twit kiye gaye vah unhone nahin kiye the or ve puri tarah galat the
 i understand that the people associated with this have suffered because of those tweets and i personally apologize to them for this
 main media se guzarish karata hum ki samvedansheeltaa dikhaaen or is maamle ko sansanikhej na banaaen
 Thanks for all of your cooperation
 " 6
 ek tamil channel se baat karte hue suchithra ne daawa kiya ki unka or karthik kaa talaak ho rahaa he or unki marji ke bina unhen aspataal le jaaya gaya tha
 He said, "karthik is a very good person
 unamem bhagwaan ram ke gun hai
 i know we are getting divorced
 isse jude sabhi logon ke liye yah dukhad he lekin kabhi na sulajhane vaali samasyaon kii vajah se ham aisa kar rahe hai
 i was in the hospital
 mujhe jabardastee aspataal le jaaya gaya tha
 " 7
 Superstar Rajinikanth's son-in-law Dhanush has not yet responded to Suchitra's tweet
 lekin unki bahan vimala gita ne is sambandh main fasebuk par ek post kiya tha jisamen likhaa tha, "twitor ek aisa madhyam ban chukaa he jahaan koi bhi kuch bhi kah saktaa he, kuch bhi post kar saktaa he
 It is sad to see that fake porn videos are posted on a platform where 12-year-olds also have an account
 or sabase bura yah he ki log aise video kii maang karte hai
 "they have now deactivated all their social media accounts
 8
 Pictures of singer Chinmayi Shripada were also posted under # Suchileaks
 unhone ek ke baad ek kai twit karke is baat kii jaankaree di ki suchithra ke pati karthik ne unhen bataaya ki suchithra kii haalat thik nahin he or vah ek bhavuk daur se guzar rahi hai
 He also said that everything going on in Suchitra's account is wrong
 unhone yah bhi likhaa ki suchithra ne unhen block kar diya he or unka consience clear he
 9
 haalanki anya sitaron ne is maamle main chinmayi kii tarah suchithra kaa saath nahin diya
 Actor-director p Samutirakani tweeted, "somebody needs mental improvement and treatment
 abhinaytaon or abhinetriyon ke naam or izzat ko nuksaan pahunchane kii anaavashyak koshish
 Use social media properly
 "tippaniyan 10
 south indian artist association ke adhyaksh abhinayta vishaal ne kaha, " jo video or photo post kiye gaye hai ve phek hai
 We are finding out who uploaded them
 suchithra kaa ilaaj chal rahaa he
 " dhanush ne haal hi main film power pandi kii shooting samaapt kii he, unhone is film kaa nirdesan kiya he

 is film main abhinetri kaajol bhi mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaa rahi hai

 3
 kuch twits main suchithra ne paroksh rup se apane saathiyon par casting couch kaa bhi aarope lagaaya
 4
 suchithra ke pati karthik, jo ek stand ap kamedian or abhinayta hai, ne apane fasebuk pej par ek video post karte hue kaha ki acount hack nahin hua he
 He said, "it shows what emotional state he is in and all of us in the family are doing everything possible to overcome him
" " unhone media se guzarish kii ki ve suchithra ko vaise treet karen jaise parivaar ke kisi sadsy ko kiya jaataa he
 The video was later removed
 5
 In place of this video of Karthik, a post was shared on his Facebook page in which he said, "as a family, the last few days were very difficult for us as Suchitra's Twitter account was hacked
 aaj hamane unka acount ritrive kar liya he
 He did not make any tweets from his account in the last few days and they were completely wrong
 main samajhataa hum ki isse jude logon ko un twits kii vajah se pareshaaniyon kaa saamana karnaa padaa or main vyaktigat rup se unase is baat ke liye maafee maangata hum
 i request the media to show sensitivity and not sensationalize the matter
 aap sabhi ke sahyog ke liye shukriya
 " 6
 Speaking to a Tamil channel, Suchitra claimed that she and Karthik were getting divorced and were taken to the hospital without her consent
 unhone kaha, "karthik bahut achche insaan hai
 They have the qualities of Lord Rama
 main jaanati hum ki ham talaak le rahe hai
 It is sad for all the people associated with it, but we are doing it because of problems that are not solved
 main aspataal main thi
 i was forced to the hospital
 " 7
 superstar rajnikant ke damaad dhanush ne suchithra ke twit par ab tak koi pratikriya nahin di he
 But her sister Vimala Geeta did a post on Facebook in this regard, which wrote, "twitter has become a medium where anyone can say anything, post anything
 yah dekhnaa dukhad he ki ek aise plateform par jahaan 12 saal ke bacchon kaa bhi acount he, phek porn video post kiye jate hai
 And the worst is that people demand such videos
 " unhone ab apane sabhi soshal media acount dactivet kar liye hai
 8
 gayika chinmayi shripada kii tasviren bhi # Suchileaks ke tahat post kii gai thim
 She informed several tweets one by one that Suchitra's husband Karthik told them that Suchitra's condition was not good and she was going through an emotional phase
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki suchithra ke acount main jo kuch bhi chal rahaa he vah galat he
 He also wrote that Suchitra has blocked him and his conscience is clear

 unhone likhaa ki un mithkon ko bhul jaaiye ki narendra modi ek taanashaah, ekadhikaaravaadi netaa hai
 The government's reversal on the Land Acquisition Bill seems to be a scared and retreating leader instead of fighting
 pradhanmantri ne ek tarah se aatm samparn kar diya
 They seem to be happier in making slogans, rather than implementing their decisions
 inhen swaminathan ayyar ne modi sarkaar ke saal puraa hone par likhaa tha ki modi ne bhrashtachar khatm kar diya he
 Because Modi has kept distance from all those business men who can no longer influence the Prime Minister from the appointment of bank chairman to the transfer of officers
 manmohan singh jab pradhanmantri the to kaha jaataa tha ki political piem nahin hai
 The country needs a political PM like Modi
 shuukravaar ko pradhanmantri chennai main the
 On the occasion of National Handloom Day
 unhone apane nijee acount se ek video twit kiya he vankkam chennai kehete hue
 In this video, the love of the people who have welcomed him is not only visible, but you can also see people from the eyes of the Prime Minister
 hamaare purv sahyogi brijmohan singh ne twit kiya ki tabhi piem ko reporter kii zarurat nahin padati he
 Our politics has indeed changed
 aaj hi dilli ke up mukhyamantri manish sisodiya ne khabar di he ki raashtrapati 4 sitambar ko dilli ke ek skool main shikshak ke rup main pesh honge
 Last year, the Prime Minister changed the entire pattern of Teacher's Day
 kahin shikshak diwas event manageron ke liye mukaable main na badal jaae
 In Chennai, the Prime Minister said on Friday that the appeal to buy Khadi on 2 October last year has been affected
 ab mujhe bataaya gaya he ki pichley saal kii tulana main 2 oktober se ab tak khaadi kii bikri 60 pratishat bad gai he
 a 60 percent increase is not a common occurrence
 press information beuro kii site par laghu or madhyam udyog mantralay kii ek press relise mili
 Of 23 July 2015
 iske anusaar khaadi gramodyog bhawan ne april, may or june 2014 kii timahi main 57 karod kii bikri kii thi
 Whereas in the same quarter of 2015, sales reached around 70 crores
 yani 2014 kii timahi kii tulana main 23 pratishat kii badhottaree hui he
 The comments piaibi par maujuud mantralay kii press relies ke anusaar 2013-14 main khaadi kii cell 1081 karod kii thi
 1144 crores in 2014-15
 ye chah pratishat he yaa saath pratishat
 The press release of 7 May 2015 stated that the Kurti Pajama Exhibition was organized in Delhi by Khadi Gramodyog Bhavan under the leadership of Minister of Small and Medium Industries Kalraj Mishra after the Prime Minister's appeal to the mind
 13 se 28 april tak lagi pradarshnee main pichley saal ke mukaable 60 pratishat kii record bikri hui he
 The sale of readymade garment has increased by 86%
 hamaara aankada puraa nahin he kyonki ham 2 oktober se ab tak koi samgr data nahin juta sake
 Khadi products also fall into different categories
 16 june ko kendriya mantri calraj mishra ne bhi 60 pratishat kii vruddhi kaa bayaan diya tha or 23 july ko kaha ki khaadi kaa cell dabl ho gaya he
 Khadi cell growth up to 60 percent cannot be a normal occurrence
 agar ye baat sahi he to kya aalochakon ko pradhanmantri ke netritv kii ye sab khubiyaan nahin dikhti hai
 So is the Modi government really shining? kya aalochak unke saath ninsaphi kar rahe hai yaa vaaki aisa kuch ho rahaa he jis par pradhanmantri ko dhyaan dena chahie
 Rahul Bajaj said that in May 2014, we got a emperor and in the last 20-30 years, in any country of the world, nobody had such success
 main is sarkaar ke virodh main aaj bhi nahin hum lekin sachai yahi he ki ab is sarkaar kii chamak feeki padati ja rahi he
 Rahul Bajaj said that he is saying what the rest of the people are saying
 bajaj ne kaha ki ye narendra modi kii sarkaar nahin he
 In Friday's Indian Express, political thinker Pratap Bhanu Mehta's article said that Prime Minister Modi's action seems to be exactly the opposite of the myths made about him
 pratap ne likhaa he ki pradhanmantri main saahas kii jagah dabbupan nazar aa rahaa he
 The government has not taken a single policy decision that can be called bold
 lage ki ve rajnatik jokhim uthaakar bhi faisla le rahe hai
 Whatever the government said on the land acquisition bill is now backing down
 is pradhanmantri kii to sari daavedaari kaam kar dikhaane kii thi
 None of his plans seem to be implemented concretely
 svachh bharat ho yaa niti ayog
 His political leadership is not visible in Parliament
 vipaksh ke khilaaf public main jaakar nahin lard rahe hai
 The feeling of neglect is coming out
 samvaad kii jagah chuppi nazar aa rahi he
 Not speaking on key issues
 vyaapman or cricket ko lekar hiton ke takaraav ne sarkaar ko chup kara diya he
 Pratap Bhanu Mehta says that it should not happen that India gets to see another Prime Minister, but he is missing
 pratap bhanu mehta se pehle 5 agast ko iconomic times main swaminathan es anclesaria ayyar kaa lekh mujhe kuch jagahon par atirek or naahak sakhti kaa shikaar laga
 He wrote that forget those myths that Narendra Modi is a dictator, monopolistic leader
 bhoomi adhigrahan bill par sarkaar ke palatney se lagata he ki ve ek dare hue or ladane kii bajaay peeche hatane vaale netaa lagate hai
 The Prime Minister surrendered in a way
 lagata he ki ve slogan banane main zyaada khush hai, bajaae apane faislon ko lagu karne main
 The same Swaminathan Iyer wrote at the end of the Modi government's year that Modi has ended corruption
 kyonki modi ne un sab bijanes main se duuri banaai he jo ab bank chairman kii niyukti se lekar adhikariyon ke tabadale ke liye pradhanmantri ko prabhavit nahin kar sakate hai
 When Manmohan Singh was Prime Minister, it was said that there is no political PM
 desh ko modi jaisaa political piem chahie
 The Prime Minister was in Chennai on Friday
 rashtriya handloom diwas ke maukey par
 He has tweeted a video from his personal account saying Vanakkam Chennai
 is video main unke swaagat main aae logon kaa pyaar to dikh hi rahaa he saath hi aap pradhanmantri kii nazar se bhi logon ko dekh sakate hai
 Our former colleague Brijmohan Singh tweeted that only then PM does not need a reporter
 hamaari raajnneeti vaaki badal gai he
 Today, Delhi Deputy Chief Minister Manish Sisodia has reported that the President will appear as a teacher in a Delhi school on 4 September
 pichley saal pradhanmantri ne shikshak diwas kii puri paripati hi badal di thi
 Nowhere does Teacher's Day turn into a match for event managers
 chennai main pradhanmantri ne shuukravaar kaha ki pichley saal 2 oktober ko khaadi kharidne kii apil kaa asar hua he
 Now i am told that Khadi sales have increased by 60 percent since October 2 as compared to last year
 60 pratishat kii vruddhi saamaanya ghatana nahin he
 a press release of the Ministry of Small and Medium Industries was found on the site of the Press Information Bureau
 23 july 2015 kii
 Accordingly, Khadi Gramodyog Bhavan had sold 57 crore in the quarter of April, May and June 2014
 jabaki 2015 kii isi timahi main bikri kareeb 70 karod tak ja pahunchi
 This means an increase of 23 percent over the 2014 quarter
 tippaniyan According to the press release of the ministry present on PIB, Khadi cell stood at Rs 1081 crore in 2013-14
 2014-15 main 1144 karod kii ho gai
 It is six percent or sixty percent
 7 may 2015 ke press relies main kaha gaya he ki pradhanmantri ke man kii baat kii apil ke baad laghu evam madhyam udyog ke mantri calraj mishra ke netritv main khaadi gramodyog bhawan ne dilli main kurta pajama pradarshnee lagi thi
 The exhibition, which took place from April 13 to 28, recorded a 60 percent record sales over the previous year
 redimaid garment kii cell to 86 percent bad gai he
 Our data is not complete as we have not been able to gather any aggregate data since October 2
 khaadi ke utpaada bhi alag-alag shrenee ke hote hai
 On 16 June, Union Minister Kalraj Mishra also gave a statement of 60 percent increase and on 23 July said that Khadi's cell has doubled
 khaadi kaa cell 60 pratishat bad jaae saamaanya ghatana nahin ho sakati
 If this is true, do the critics not see all these characteristics of the Prime Minister's leadership
 to kya vaaki modi sarkaar kii chamak feeki padane lagi he
 Are critics criticizing them or is there really something that the Prime Minister should pay attention to
 shuukravaar ke indian express main raajnneetik chintak pratap bhanu mehta ke lekh main kaha he ki pradhanmantri modi kaa ection unhen lekar bane mithkon se thik ulta nazar aa rahaa he
 Pratap has written that in the Prime Minister, the place of courage is being seen
 sarkaar ne ek bhi aisa nitigat faisla nahin liya he jise bold kaha ja sake
 It seems that they are taking a decision even after taking political risks
 bhoomi adhigrahan bill par sarkaar ne jo bhi kaha ab usee se peeche hat rahi he
 This prime minister had to show all the claim
 unki koi bhi yojana thos rup se lagu hoti nazar nahin aa rahi he
 Clean India or NITI Aayog
 sansad main unka rajnatik netritv nahin dikh rahaa he
 They are not fighting against the opposition by going public
 bechaargi kaa bhav hi saamne aa rahaa he
 There is silence in place of dialogue
 mukhya muddon par bol nahin rahe hai
 Conflict of interest over business and cricket has silenced the government
 pratap bhanu mehta kehete hai ki kahin aisa na ho jaae ki bharat ko ek or aisa pradhanmantri dekhne ko mil jaae to dikhte hai magar gumshuda hai

 ‚Äô Life is punctuated with a series of memorable moments: your first day at the workplace, the day you get married, that moment when you hold your baby in your arms, the day when your child graduates, your retirement day
 
 
 the list is endless
 We need to be financially prepared at each phase to ensure that we can enjoy each of these special moments in life without much worry
 To ensure you are prepared for all life stage requirements and ensure your family is well protected in case of unforeseen circumstances, one needs life insurance plans that help you your future well and also provide protection to your loved ones
 Depending on the type of life insurance policy you choose, you can build a corpus for life's important milestones such as children's birth, education, marriage, plan for your post-retirement years
 What also is of paramount importance is to secure your family's financial future, should anything unfortunate were to happen
 The earlier you factor in life insurance in your financial planning, the better it is
 Here's how insurance can benefit you at every stage of life
 Unmarried young adults: You have just passed out of college and got yourself a dream job that promises you a fat pay cheque
 This is the time you should not lose sight of your goals
 You must judiciously plan your finances in such a way that apart from securing your present, you're covered for the future too
 Life insurance lets you do just that
 It acts as a safety net in times of crisis
 Once you are married, it will help you secure the future of your spouse and kids
 The biggest advantage of life insurance is that it is financially beneficial in the long run
 The younger you are when you buy insurance, the more affordable your premium will be
 Not to forget the tax benefits that you can avail through a life insurance policy
 Newly married:the very thought of sharing your life with a loved one is exciting and that's what makes marriage so special
 It is only natural then that you would want to lead a secure and comfortable life with your spouse
 In the wake of additional expenses and responsibilities that marriage brings along, it is necessary to make changes to your financial plan
 a life insurance policy can go a long way in securing the financial future of your family
 From providing regular returns during your lifetime to taking care of your family's financial needs in case of any eventuality, life insurance has multifold benefits
 Married with kids: Parenthood marks the beginning of a wonderful phase in any person's life
 Your world revolves around your child and you would want the best for him or her
 You follow every growth milestone of your child with love and fondness
 During this exciting phase, somewhere at the back of your mind, you also keep thinking about the future of your child - school, college, higher studies and even marriage
 You think of ways you can prepare yourself financially to meet all these requirements
 Choosing the right life insurance plan will simplify things for you
 As a new parent, you can build a corpus over a period of time for your kids' education and marriage
 Likewise, in case of any unfortunate event, the insurance amount will ensure that the future of your children is not negatively impacted and they can fulfill all their dreams
 Retirees: Years roll by
 While your children have settled down and are now busy with their own lives, you are all set to enter the most interesting phase of your life - the post-retirement period
 Gone are the days when retirement meant idling away reading newspapers while sipping tea
 These days, retirees look forward to making the most of the golden period of their lives
 Be it holidays around the world or trying their hand at new activities, they want to live their lives to the fullest
 And for all this, parents wouldn't want to financially depend on their children
 Opting for a life insurance plan, that offers retirement solutions, early on in life will be of great help during your retirement years
 It will help you lead a comfortable post-retirement life
 Besides, old age is often characterized by fragile health
 As a result, there can be many unplanned expenses too
 Your insurance policy will provide for those as well
 Now that you have identified yourself as part of one of the above groups, make sure you choose the right life insurance policy
 Protecting you for life From affordable term insurance plans to monthly income plans, Bharti AXA Lifehas solutions that suits you irrespective of the group you belong to
 Their insurance plans are designed to financially protect you and your family
 The company also offers an online term insurance plan for those who wish to directly buy a policy
 You also understand that this relationship is long-term and a key point of expectation is the claims management process
 At the time of claims settlement, Bharti AXA Lifeprovides you services of dedicated claims handler who will help with the claims process
 From explaining the finer points to assisting with paperwork, the claims handler will be with the beneficiary throughout
 This will not only quicken the claims process, but also lend a personal touch to it
 This way, with life insurance, you can meet all your financial goals at different life-stages and also secure your family's future

 varsh 1998 se ghudsavaar police main nayi bhartee nahin hui he
